 Labor Day or May Day is celebrated every year on May 1 (1 May) around the world
 is din desh kii lagbhag sabhi companiyon main chuttee rahati he
 Not only India, this day is a national holiday in about 80 countries of the world
 bharat main majdoor diwas (labour Day In India) kaamkaaji logon ke sammaan main manaaya jaataa he
 The first day of celebrating Labor Day in India started in Chennai on 1 May 1923
 us samay isko madras diwas ke taur par pramanit kar liya gaya tha
 It was started by Comrade Singaravelu Chettiar, leader of the Bharatiya Mazdoor Kisan Party

 shahbaaj nadeem ne do ran ke kul yoga par akshat reddy (1) ko ran out karke dairedevills ko manamafik shuruyaat dilaai lekin iske baad parthiv patel (19) or captain kumaar sangakaara (28) ne duusare wicket ke liye 44 ran jodakar is gam ko kam kiya
 Parthiv was caught at the hands of Nadeem on a total of 46 runs
 parthiv ne 19 gendon par chaar chauke lagaae
 After this Sangakkara took the score to 54 with Hanuma Vihari (17) but on this sum, Johan Botha dismissed Sangakkara and returned his team to the match again
 ab dairedevills ke paas match par pakad banane kaa mauka tha
 To cash in on the occasion, Nadeem stumps Cameron White (4) at the hands of Kedar Jadhav for a total of 69 runs
 white kaa wicket 14wein over kii antim gend par gira
 Morne Morkel gave Vihari the fifth ball from the second ball of the 15th over, giving his team a fifth success
 iske baad ashish reddy (16) umesh yadav ke over main do chauke lagaakar apni team ko phir se waapas match main laae lekin morkal dwaara phenke gaye 17wein over kii pehali gend par vah ek galat shot khilne ke prayaas main bold ho gaye
 Mishra took eight runs, including a no ball in that over of Morkel, to take the figure to 18 runs from 18 balls until its completion
 duusare chor par thisira perera sirf do gend khelkar apni baari ke intjaar main the
 Famous for playing big shots, Perera had faced only two balls so far
 irfan pathan dwaara phenke gaye 18wein over kii pehali gend par dairedevills team ne mishra par jaanboojh kar wicket kii ore thro kii gai gend ke raste main aane kaa aarope lagaaya lekin ampaire aleem daar ne ise nakaar diya
 After the second ball went empty, Mishra took a run on the third ball and thus Perera returned on strike
 perera ne pathan kii gend ko long aan ke upar se udaane kaa prayaas kiya lekin vah bilkul seemaa rekha par botha ke dwaara lapke gaye
 He could score only two runs
 unka wicket 100 ran ke kul yoga par gira
 The Sunrisers were to score 12 runs off the final 12 balls
 mishra or del sten ne ek chauke kii madad se is over main chah ran liye
 In this way, the Sunrisers needed six runs to win in the last over
 yah over irfan lekar aae
 On the first ball, Stan scored two runs and hit a four off the second ball to ensure his team's victory
 dairedevills kii ore se nadeem or morkal ne do-do safalataa hasil kii
 Botha and Pathan got one wicket each
 isse pehle, toss jeetne ke baad pehle ballebaaji karne utari dairedevills team apane teen diggajon-david warner, virendra sahvaag or captain mahela jayavardhane kii naakaami ke kaaran nirdhaarit 20 overon main aath wicket par 114 ran hi bana saki
 Kedar Jadhav scored the most unbeaten 30 runs while Irfan Pathan contributed 23 runs
 warner khaataa bhi nahin khol sake jabaki sahvaag or jayavardhane 12-12 ran hi bana sake
 The host team had a very poor start
 sabase pehle warner (0) vidaa hue
 Sunrisers' South African Express Dale Steyn showed Warner the way to the pavilion on the fourth ball of the innings
 iske baad laga ki sahvaag or jayavardhane is nuksaan kii bharpai kar denge
 The duo added 26 runs for the second wicket but Ishant Sharma proved Jayawardene on the third ball of the fifth over and Sehwag on the fourth ball to prove that he was no longer Sehwag but Delhi's domineering
 sahvaag ne 10 gendon par do chauke lagaae jabaki captain 14 gendon par ek chaukaa or ek chakka lagaakar out hue
 After this, Johan Botha (9) and Manpreet Juneja (15) brought the score to 44 runs, but on the same sum, Anand Rajan dismissed Delhi to give the fourth blow
 juneja or irfan ne paanchaven wicket ke liye 21 ranon kii saajhedaari kar sthiti ko sambhaalane kii koshish kii lekin 65 ranon ke kul yoga par amit mishra ne juneja ko camran white ke haathon kaich kara diya
 Juneja faced 22 balls
 pathan or jadhav par ab team kaa kul yoga 100 ke paar pahunchane kii jimmedaari thi
 Both tried hard for this but Pathan was dismissed at a total of 95
 donon ke bich 30 ranon kii saajhedaari hui

 thisira perera ne pathan ko hanuma vihari ke haathon kaich karaayaa
 Perera then dismissed Morne Morkel (0) on a total of 96
 tippaniyan The right-handed Qasar Stein completed the second ball of the 19th over of the innings by bowling Shehzad Nadeem (0)
 yah wicket 98 ke kul yoga par gira

 iske baad haalanki jadhav or yadav ne koi or nuksaan nahin hone diya or antim wicket ke liye 16 ran jode
 Jadhav hit one four and two sixes off 20 balls
 sunrisers kii ore se ishanth, perera or sten ne do-do wicket liye jabaki rajan or mishra ko ek-ek safalataa mili
 This low-scoring match was made difficult by the Sunrisers batsmen due to their poor batting
 yahi kaaran he ki unhen tamaam prayaason ke baad 20wein over main saat wicket ganvaakar jeet mili
 Dale Steyn, returning David Warner to the pavilion on the fourth ball of the innings, hit the winning four
 sten nau ranon par naabad rahe jabaki amit mishra ek ahm pari khelte hue 16 ranon par naabad laute
 Mishra hit two fours off 14 balls
 dairedevills kii tarah sunrisers kii shuruyaat bhi acchhee nahin rahi thi

 is maukey ko bhunaate hue nadeem ne 69 ranon ke kul yoga par camran white (4) ko kedaar jadhav ke haathon stump karaayaa

 morne morkal ne 15wein over kii duusari gend par vihari ko botha ke haathon kaich karakar apni team ko paanchavin safalataa dilaai
 Ashish Reddy (16) then brought his team back into the match again with two fours in Umesh Yadav's over but he was bowled in the first ball of the 17th over bowled by Morkel in an attempt to play a wrong shot
 mishra ne morkal ke us over main ek no ball sahit aath ran lekar isaki samaapti tak aankade ko 18 gendon par 18 ranon tak pahunchaa diya

 bade shots khilne ke liye mashhoor perera ne ab tak sirf do gendon kaa saamana kiya tha

 duusari gend khaali jane ke baad teesri gend par mishra ne ek ran liya or is tarah perera strike par laute

 warner khaataa bhi nahin khol sake jabaki sahvaag or jayavardhane 12-12 ran hi bana sake
 The host team had a very poor start
 sabase pehle warner (0) vidaa hue
 Sunrisers' South African Express Dale Steyn showed Warner the way to the pavilion on the fourth ball of the innings
 iske baad laga ki sahvaag or jayavardhane is nuksaan kii bharpai kar denge
 The duo added 26 runs for the second wicket but Ishant Sharma proved Jayawardene on the third ball of the fifth over and Sehwag on the fourth ball to prove that he was no longer Sehwag but Delhi's domineering
 sahvaag ne 10 gendon par do chauke lagaae jabaki captain 14 gendon par ek chaukaa or ek chakka lagaakar out hue
 After this, Johan Botha (9) and Manpreet Juneja (15) brought the score to 44 runs, but on the same sum, Anand Rajan dismissed Delhi to give the fourth blow
 juneja or irfan ne paanchaven wicket ke liye 21 ranon kii saajhedaari kar sthiti ko sambhaalane kii koshish kii lekin 65 ranon ke kul yoga par amit mishra ne juneja ko camran white ke haathon kaich kara diya
 Juneja faced 22 balls
 pathan or jadhav par ab team kaa kul yoga 100 ke paar pahunchane kii jimmedaari thi
 Both tried hard for this but Pathan was dismissed at a total of 95
 donon ke bich 30 ranon kii saajhedaari hui
 Pathan hit a four off 30 balls
 thisira perera ne pathan ko hanuma vihari ke haathon kaich karaayaa
 Perera then dismissed Morne Morkel (0) on a total of 96
 tippaniyan The right-handed Qasar Stein completed the second ball of the 19th over of the innings by bowling Shehzad Nadeem (0)
 yah wicket 98 ke kul yoga par gira
 Steyn bowled the most economical IPL-6 so far, taking two wickets for 11 runs including a maiden in four overs
 iske baad haalanki jadhav or yadav ne koi or nuksaan nahin hone diya or antim wicket ke liye 16 ran jode
 Jadhav hit one four and two sixes off 20 balls
 sunrisers kii ore se ishanth, perera or sten ne do-do wicket liye jabaki rajan or mishra ko ek-ek safalataa mili
 Mishra took eight runs, including a no ball in that over of Morkel, to take the figure to 18 runs from 18 balls until its completion
 duusare chor par thisira perera sirf do gend khelkar apni baari ke intjaar main the
 Famous for playing big shots, Perera had faced only two balls so far
 irfan pathan dwaara phenke gaye 18wein over kii pehali gend par dairedevills team ne mishra par jaanboojh kar wicket kii ore thro kii gai gend ke raste main aane kaa aarope lagaaya lekin ampaire aleem daar ne ise nakaar diya
 After the second ball went empty, Mishra took a run on the third ball and thus Perera returned on strike
 perera ne pathan kii gend ko long aan ke upar se udaane kaa prayaas kiya lekin vah bilkul seemaa rekha par botha ke dwaara lapke gaye

 unka wicket 100 ran ke kul yoga par gira

 " Elections are being campaigned in Maharashtra through dubious international numbers on whatsapp
 maharashtra main vidhansabha chunaav se thik pehle onnaline prachaar ne teji pakad lee he
 Political parties are making full use of social networking sites like whatsapp to reach people, but the shocking thing is that the messages on whatsapp have started coming from international numbers
 is vakt maharashtra ke mahaasangram main sabhi rajnatik partiyaan har tareeke kii ranneeti apana rahi he, jisamen mobile prachaar bhi shaamil he
 According to technical experts, some political parties have spent crores of rupees and have taken international servers, through which they are sending their favorite election message to crores of people of Maharashtra
 dikhne main yah number aam number jaisaa hota he
 At first glance, it will look as if someone sitting abroad has sent this message, but in reality the number belongs to the international server
 iti visheshgy devang dave ne kaha, 'ye number antarrashtriya sarwar ke hai
 Most of the messages that are circulating on whatsapp are being sent from international servers so that no one can call back and check
 devang kii maane to yah antarrashtriya sarwar raajnneetik partiyon ne kharid rakhe hai, jisase vah apni party kaa prachaar karne ke saath saamne vaali party kii buraai bhi aasaani se kar sake
 According to internet guru Vijay Mukhi, 'the entire payment for purchasing international servers is through hawala
 ye sarwar desh ke baahar hote hai, lekin ise bharat se hi chalaaya jaataa he
 Overall, if the message comes from a mobile number on whatsapp, the police or election officer can check the owner of that mobile if needed, but it is very difficult to check if the number is from an international server

 konchita ne davis cap kii taiyaariyon main juty spanish team ke abhyaas satr ke dauraan buudhvaar ko ieenes ko die saakshaatkaar main kaha, "main tennis main sakriy rahane ke dauraan yadi or khitaab jeet paati to acha rahata
 i won Wimbledon while playing, though i wanted to win more Grand Slam titles
 " Konchita said, "but now i have become a coach
 main ek khilaadi ke taur par jitani safal rahi usase kahin adhik safalataa bataur coach arjeet karnaa chaahati hum
 Our main goal is to return to the Davis Cup World Group and hope to win the Davis Cup title as well
 " The 44-year-old Conchita has also been appointed as the non-competitive captain of Spain's Fed Cup and she is enjoying her career as a coach these days
 konchita ne kaha, "yah bilkul juda ahsaas he
 Now i know that my return as a player is not possible, so i am enjoying my responsibilities as a coach
 hamaare paas rafel nadal or david pherar jaise dhurandhar khilaadiyon se las behtareen team he, jisase meraa kaam kaaphi aasaan ho jaataa he
 " haalanki konchita ne yah bhi sweekaar kiya ki bharat ke khilaaf davis cap main khelte hue spanish khilaadiyon ko dilli kii garmi pareshaan karegi
 At the same time, he also expressed happiness over the hard work of his team's players who are rapidly adapting themselves in the Indian environment during practice
 unhone kaha, "yahaan kaa vaataavaran kaaphi kathin he
 We are not so hot, but we are happy with our practice
 yahaan tennis court vastav main kaaphi achche hai
 i am happy that the players of my team are fast adapting themselves according to the environment and court here
 "tippaniyan The Spanish team has been out of the Davis Cup World Group for the last few years and has also lost to Brazil and Germany in the World Group playoff matches
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) konchita 1994 main wimbledon main mahila ekal varg kii champion rah chuki hai, jahaan unhone america diggaj martina navaratilova ko final main maat di thi
 In addition, she was runner-up at the Australian Open in 1998 and the French Open in 2000
 bharat ke khilaaf davis cap world group plaof muqabla khilne ai spanish team kii gaiyr-pratispardhi captain evam purv duusari vishwa variyata praapt konchita ab bataur coach safalataa arjeet karnaa chaahati hai
 "I would have been better if i could have won more titles while i was active in tennis," Conchita said in an interview to IANS on Wednesday during the Spanish team's practice session in preparation for the Davis Cup
 maine khelte hue wimbledon jeeta, haalanki main or grand slam khitaab jeetna chaahati thi
 " konchita ne kaha, "lekin ab main coach ban chuki hum
 i want to earn more success as a coach than as successful as a player
 hamaara mukhya lakshya davis cap world group main vaapasi karnaa he or ummid he ham davis cap khitaab bhi jeeten
 " 44 varshiya konchita ko spain kii fed cap kaa bhi gaiyr pratispardhi captain niyukt kiya gaya he or coach ke taur par apane kariyar kaa vah in dinon lutf uthaa rahi hai
 Konchita said, "it's a very different feeling
 ab mujhe pataa he ki khilaadi ke taur par meri vaapasi sambhav nahin he, isliye main coach kii apni jimmedaariyon kaa lutf uthaa rahi hum
 We have a great team equipped with rambunctious players like Rafael Nadal and David Ferrer, which makes my work much easier
 " However, Conchita also admitted that playing in the Davis Cup against India would upset the Spanish players in Delhi's heat
 saath hi unhone abhyaas ke dauraan teji se bhartiya vaataavaran main khud ko dhaal rahe apni team ke khilaadiyon kii mehnat par khushi bhi jaahir kii
 He said, "the climate here is quite tough
 hamen itani garmi kii aadat nahin he, lekin ham apane abhyaas ko lekar khush hai
 The tennis courts here are actually quite good
 mujhe khushi he ki meri team ke khilaadi teji se yahaan ke vaataavaran or court ke hisaab se khud ko dhaal rahe hai
 "comments spanish team beete kuch varsho se davis cap world group se baahar hi rahi he or world group plaof muqablon main bhi use brazil or germany ke haathon haar jhelni padi he

 The Left Front is going to be in power for the fifth time in the state, winning a landslide victory in Tripura Assembly
 guuruuvaar ko aae chunaav parinaam ne sabko chaunkaa diya he
 The Left Front has captured 50 of the 60 assembly seats, while the opposition Congress had to settle for just 10 seats
 chunaav parinaam saamne aane ke baad vampanthi partiyon, khaskar marxvaadi communist party (makapa) ke kaaryakarta puure rajya main utsav manaa rahe hai, jabaki congress ke kheme main sannata pasra hua he
 The CPI (M) won 49 seats, while its ally Communist Party of India (CPI) won one seat
 1978 ke baad vam morcha ke liye is baar kaa parinaam behatar sabit hua he
 In 1978, the Morcha won 56 seats
 2008 ke vidhansabh chunaav ke mukaable morcha ne is baar ek seat zyada jiti he
 Pleased with the victory, Chief Minister Manik Sarkar said, “people voted in favor of good governance apart from development, peace and stability
 " Manik Sarkar, 64, who has been ruling the state since 1998, has won the Dhanpur seat for the sixth time
 ve akele aise netaa hai jo chauthi baar tripura ke mukhyamantri pad par kabiz honge
 While the Congress managed to retain only 10 seats, its ally Indigenous Nationalist Party of Tripura (INPT) has been disappointed
 paanch saal pehle isane ek seat par jeet hasil kii thi
 The Trinamool Congress fielded 22 candidates in 2008, but it did not field a single candidate in this election to prevent the division of non-lf votes
 uske 'baikfoot' par jane kaa bhi haalanki congress ko phayda nahin mil paaya
 The comments shikshak se rajaneta bane 75 varshiya anil sarkaar kavi or lekhak bhi hai
 He set the record by winning the election for the ninth time
 vah makapa ke tikat par pashchimi tripura ke pratapgarh se phir nirvaachit hue hai
 It is noteworthy that the Left Front has been in power in Tripura since 1978
 yah morcha sirf ek baar (1988-93 ke dauraan) satta se dur rahaa tha
 Workers of leftist parties, especially the Communist Party of india-marxist (CPI-M), have been celebrating across the state after the election results came out, while the Congress camp was silent
 makapa ne 49 siton par jeet darj kii, jabaki uski sahyogi bhartiya communist party (bhakpa) ne ek seat par jeet hasil kii he
 This result has proved to be better for the Left Front after 1978
 1978 main morcha ne 56 siton par jeet hasil kii thi
 The Morcha has won one seat more this time than in the 2008 assembly elections
 jeet se prasann mukhyamantri maanik sarkaar ne kaha, "logon ne vikaas, shanti or sthayitv ke alaava sushasan ke paksh main matdaan kiya
 " varsh 1998 se hi rajya main shashan chalaa rahe 64 varshiya maanik sarkaar dhanpur seat se chhathi baar jite hai
 He is the only leader who will hold the post of Chief Minister of Tripura for the fourth time
 congress jahaan maatr 10 siten barkaraar rakhane main kaamyaab rahi, vahiin uski sahyogi indiinas nesanalist party of tripura (aienpiti) ko niraashaa haath lagi he
 It won one seat five years ago
 trinmul congress ne 2008 main 22 pratyaashee maidan main utaare the, lekin gaiyr vaamo maton ke vibhaajan ko rokane ke liye is baar ke chunaav main usne ek bhi pratyaashee khadaa nahin kiya
 However, the Congress did not get the benefit of going to its 'backfoot'
 tippaniyan 75-year-old teacher-turned-politician Anil Sarkar is also a poet and writer
 unhone nauveen baar chunaav jitkar record kaayam kiya
 He has been re-elected from Pratapgarh in western Tripura on a CPI-M ticket
 ullekhneey he ki tripura main vam morcha 1978 se hi satta par kabiz he
 This front had been away from power only once (during 1988–93)
